  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_51854387-a1d3-4d56-a22e-8a7ca2397110'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };
    if (typeof AppleID !== "undefined") {
      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();
    }

<div id="review_2836255720" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2836255720" />
    <a title="Darian Ramos" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/97079329-darian-ramos"><img alt="Darian Ramos" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1558664204p2/97079329.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2836255720?book_show_action=true">May 27, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Darian Ramos" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Darian Ramos" href="/user/show/97079329-darian-ramos">Darian Ramos</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9788408114512" href="/book/show/33857532-good-morning-princess">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
                  <em>
                    This review has been hidden because it contains spoilers. To view it,
                    <a href="#" onclick="Effect.toggle(&#39;reviewTextContainer2836255720&#39;); return false;">click here.</a>
                  </em>
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2836255720" class="readable"
                    style="display:none"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11710749556063916126">Okay, First, it's the first book I read of Blue Jeans. Continue:<br/><br/>I like the plot, it's different and interesting, the characters are intelligent, different and complex, not all, but the majority. My principal problem with this book it's the romance, I don't Liked... Because it's, in my opinion, toxic, fake, and... wow, very complicated. But, I'm talking about the good points of this book first.<br/><br/>Good Points:<br/><br/>The plot it's good, toxic but good. Why?, because it's talking about the "frikis" (In my cou</span>
  <span id="freeText11710749556063916126" style="display:none">Okay, First, it's the first book I read of Blue Jeans. Continue:<br /><br />I like the plot, it's different and interesting, the characters are intelligent, different and complex, not all, but the majority. My principal problem with this book it's the romance, I don't Liked... Because it's, in my opinion, toxic, fake, and... wow, very complicated. But, I'm talking about the good points of this book first.<br /><br />Good Points:<br /><br />The plot it's good, toxic but good. Why?, because it's talking about the "frikis" (In my country friki it's same to rarely) guys, they don't have friends, but the destiny take the decision to join them (Bruno, Maria, Ester, Elisabeth, Raul And Valeria). At this moment they founded The misfits Club; so in my opinion they have NOTHING misunderstood. So, the time goes fast, and they don't have the same connection. And the problem start when Bruno have feelings for Ester, Valeria and Eli for Raul, and he for Valeria, And not the least Mari for Ester. Yeah... very complicated.<br /><br />My problem it's started with Elisabeth and it's finished with Rodrigo and Cesar. <br /><br />Eli... OMG!, I'm started with she because... the hate first and the loves later. She's so fake, manipulative, okay, in a word... toxic. She's the girl than was ugly everybody hates she, but now she's "beautiful" she thinks the all boys are at her feet. But, with Raul it's different, and she can not accept he doesn't like her. So At this moment it's when she's starts to: Manipulate her best friend (yeah HER BEST FRIEND), be a harpy, dress (in a chapter) like a prostitute. And she obsessive with this guy. Yes, I know she had "mental problems" but for me, that's a bad excuse from the writer.<br /><br />My second problem it's the Relationship from Rodrigo and Ester... this's not a relationship it's a bunch of ... toxic waste. Hey, you, yes you!, you have less than fourteen or fifteen don't pay attention to that, It's NOT a relationship. Third problem, The relation with Cesar and Valeria... Don't talk to someone you know in the subway. DON'T!.<br /><br />So, go to the Love:<br /><br />Maria and Bruno, I was matching this pair.<br /><br />Maria it's so sweet, intelligent, good friend, beautiful and no, I'm not only talking about physical ( DID YOU LISTEN THAT ELI?). I think she's the only person in this book... than doesn't need a psychologist.<br /><br />Bruno in my opinion, it's better for Ester, MUCH BETTER!. He's a good boy, had problems with his family but hey it's normal, tell me, what's teenager doesn't have problem with his family in this age?.<br /><br />And now... my favorite Character: Alicia.<br /><br />OMG... she's the villain, and I love for that. She's the mastermind in the problems for Eli, She's a friend and enemy. She's the most interesting of all characters.<br /><br /><br />So this's my opinion, I'm going to read the second book because I don't want this to end like this. And... Sorry for the mistakes, I'm not the best in this language. Thanks, For reading BYE!! ^ . ^<br /><br /> <br /><br /><br /><br /></span>

<div class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground">Readers also enjoyed</h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent"><div class='bookCarousel'>
<div class='carouselRow' style='width: 3600px'>
<ul>
<li class='cover' id='bookCover_33857530'>
<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/33857530-buenos-dias-princesa"><img alt="¡BUENOS DIAS, PRINCESA!" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/books/1484419141l/33857530._SX98_.jpg" />
</a>

  
<script type="text/javascript" charset="utf-8">
//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('ZsXyPjPC/TB5P3wwny2Q/akmo+u7BbuMtbUYl8DaxmGr3W2/GXrf4qMF6w1wplhqHtzLlbzDYvPyK9HV5eUkog==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('3pUT+KCMr2HMvaQhinUxCQ5AYOHaNEQred58WhldOoUTjYx5ijSNsxaHMxxl/vmeuboIn93ynVQ+QLUYPGLYRg==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>

Malgrado abbiano la maturità ne combinano ogni giorno di tutti i colori. Sfilate, feste, rave e tutti i possibili eventi anche fuori Roma. Alex è un &quot;ragazzo&quot; di quasi trentasette anni. Si è lasciato da poco e senza un vero perché con la sua fidanzata storica. Intorno a lui ruota un mondo complicato e divertente: i suoi genitori, le sue sorelle sposate e con figli e poi i suoi tre amici Enrico, Flavio e Pietro, anche loro tutti già sposati ma ognuno con le proprie particolarità. Enrico è geloso, Flavio metodico, Pietro invece è in fissa con tutte le donne del mondo. Alex è un pubblicitario e ha delle grandi responsabilità all\'interno della sua azienda. Ma è appena arrivato un giovane rampante che mette a repentaglio il suo lavoro. E tutto questo non sarebbe niente se quella mattina Alex non incontrasse Niki. O meglio, se i due non si scontrassero. Niki è una bella ragazza, è divertente, è intelligente, è spiritosa, è allegra. C\'è solo un piccolo dettaglio. Ha diciassette anni. Vent\'anni meno di Alex. E dopo l\'incontro di quella mattina, nulla sarà più come prima. Il mondo adulto si scontra con quello degli adolescenti. Ed ecco mamme e figlie in una discussione continua, papà che sono ancora ragazzini e ragazzi giovanissimi che sono già troppo adulti. E ancora ragazze sognatrici, ragazze deluse, ragazze romantiche e ragazze troppo folli. E adulti che invece hanno messo da parte tutti i loro sogni e vivono, o meglio sopravvivono, senza avere il coraggio di fermarsi a riflettere. Questo romanzo è la voglia di ritrovare la propria libertà, la voglia di avere sentimenti veri, di amare senza convenzioni e senza troppi perché. È la quotidianità ma è anche il sogno. È la voglia di dire basta a quel domani che ogni giorno ci raccontiamo, nel quale siamo sempre sicuri che faremo qualcosa di speciale. Ma intanto i giorni passano e quel domani non arriva. Di lui non c\'è traccia. E allora ecco la nostra fuga, la più bella, la più folle, la più pazza. Una fuga d\'amore. E poi quel faro. Insomma, un tuffo dove l\'acqua è più blu. <span id="freeTextContainer15751731698487585155">Francisco de Paula Fernández es el autor de la serie de libros Canciones para Paula, que escribe bajo el seudónimo de Blue Jeans. Nació en Sevilla, España. Estudio en los Salesianos y luego en el instituto Maese Rodrigo. Cuando termino hizo un año de Derecho en la Facultad de Sevilla. No era su vocación y decidió emprender la aventura de cambiar de carrera y de ciudad. Con 18 años viajo a Madrid y</span>
  <span id="freeText15751731698487585155" style="display:none">Francisco de Paula Fernández es el autor de la serie de libros Canciones para Paula, que escribe bajo el seudónimo de Blue Jeans. Nació en Sevilla, España. Estudio en los Salesianos y luego en el instituto Maese Rodrigo. Cuando termino hizo un año de Derecho en la Facultad de Sevilla. No era su vocación y decidió emprender la aventura de cambiar de carrera y de ciudad. Con 18 años viajo a Madrid y estudió Periodismo en la Universidad Europea. Siempre ha disfrutado de la escritura y su lenguaje llega a los adolescentes por ser actual, fresco y dinámico. Canciones para Paula fue su primera novela publicada, y que comenzó como una historia que cientos de lectores seguían a través de diferentes redes sociales en Internet. <br /><br /></span>
